K67</div></td></tr><tr class="mergedbottomrow"><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Postal Sorting Office</th><td class="infobox-data adr"><div class="postal-code">SWORDS</div></td></tr><tr class="mergedrow"><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Dialing Code</th><td class="infobox-data">+353(0)1</td></tr><tr class="mergedrow"><th scope="row" class="infobox-label"><a href="/wiki/Geocode" title="Geocode">Geocode</a></th><td class="infobox-data nickname"><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion" style="white-space: nowrap"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://geohack.toolforge.org/geohack.php?pagename=Swords,_Dublin&amp;params=53.459066514695_N_6.2182014555302_W_region:IE_scale:25000">O184469</a></span></td></tr><tr class="mergedrow"><th scope="row" class="infobox-label"><a href="/wiki/ISO_3166" title="ISO 3166">ISO 3166 code</a></th><td class="infobox-data nickname">IE-D</td></tr><tr class="mergedrow"><th scope="row" scope="row" class="infobox-label">Website</th><td class="infobox-data"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.fingal.ie/visitor/locations/swords">Swords on fingal.ie</a></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Swords</b> (<a href="/wiki/Irish_language" title="Irish language">Irish</a>: <i lang="ga">Sord</i><sup id="cite_ref-Swords_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Swords-10">&#91;N 1&#93;</a></sup> <small></small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Irish" title="Help:IPA/Irish">[s\xcb\xa0o\xcb\x90\xc9\xbe\xcb\xa0d\xcc\xaa\xcb\xa0]</a></span> or <i lang="ga" title="Irish-language text">Sord Cholmcille</i>) is the <a href="/wiki/County_town" title="County town">county town</a> of <a href="/wiki/Fingal" title="Fingal">Fingal</a> and a large suburban town in north Dublin.  Lying ten kilometres<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> north of the city centre, on the Ward River, and reputedly founded around 560 A.D., it features a restored medieval castle, a holy well from which it takes its name, a round tower and a Norman tower.  Near to <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Airport" title="Dublin Airport">Dublin Airport</a>, Swords is also home to one of the Dublin region\'s larger shopping centres, <i>The Pavilions</i>, several other retail facilities and a range of industries.  Suburban housing estates lie around the town centre, with several parks and many schools and sporting facilities.\n</p><p>The name "Swords" is also applicable to a <a href="/wiki/Townland" title="Townland">townland</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Swords_3_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Swords_3-12">&#91;N 2&#93;</a></sup> to the <a href="/wiki/Civil_parishes_in_Ireland" title="Civil parishes in Ireland">civil parish</a>, within the historic <a href="/wiki/County_Dublin" title="County Dublin">County Dublin</a>, and to the <a href="/wiki/Municipal_district_(Ireland)" class="mw-redirect" title="Municipal district (Ireland)">local electoral area</a>.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toclevel-2 tocsection-67"><a href="#Notes"><span class="tocnumber">14.1</span> <span class="toctext">Notes</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-68"><a href="#Sources"><span class="tocnumber">14.2</span> <span class="toctext">Sources</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-69"><a href="#External_links"><span class="tocnumber">15</span> <span class="toctext">External links</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Map_of_Swords.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Map_of_Swords.png/220px-Map_of_Swords.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="131" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Map_of_Swords.png/330px-Map_of_Swords.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Map_of_Swords.png/440px-Map_of_Swords.png 2x" data-file-width="1496" data-file-height="894" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Map_of_Swords.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of Swords</div></div></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Origins_and_etymology">Origins and etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Origins and etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The town\'s origins date back to 560 AD when it was reputedly founded by <a href="/wiki/Saint_Colmcille" class="mw-redirect" title="Saint Colmcille">Saint Colmcille</a> (521\xe2\x80\x93567).<sup id="cite_ref-Sidwell_70_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sidwell_70-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Legend has it that the saint blessed a local well, giving the settlement its name, <i>Sord</i>, meaning "clear" or "pure". However, <i>An Sord</i> also means "the water source" and could indicate a large communal drinking well that existed in antiquity.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> St. Colmcille\'s Well is located on Well Road off Main Street. <i>Sord</i> may also refer to a "sward", an \'expanse of grass\'.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> The most ubiquitous landscape indicators of early Christian settlement are the ecclesiastical enclosures, and in the case of Swords, the street pattern has been influenced by the circular alignment of the settlement.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Development">Development</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Development">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The medieval town developed in a linear pattern along Main Street, in a roughly north\xe2\x80\x93south direction. The <a href="/wiki/Irish_round_tower" title="Irish round tower">round tower</a>, 26m in height, is also an indicator of early Christian settlement. The <a href="/wiki/List_of_High_Kings_of_Ireland" title="List of High Kings of Ireland">Irish high king</a> <a href="/wiki/Brian_Boru" title="Brian Boru">Brian Boru</a> is said to have had his funeral at the church on Spittal Hill after he was killed at the Battle of Clontarf; this was of course before the hospital and even the Church of Ireland when there would have been a small chapel there along with the round tower. \n</p><p>At the northern end of the street stands Swords Castle, 200m northeast of the ecclesiastical site, which was built in the early 13th century. A short distance north of the castle is the elevation known as Spittal Hill, where a hospital once stood.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Modern_times">Modern times</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Modern times">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In 1994, Swords became the <a href="/wiki/County_town" title="County town">county seat</a> of the new county of <a href="/wiki/Fingal" title="Fingal">Fingal</a> after the abolition of the former <a href="/wiki/County_Dublin" title="County Dublin">County Dublin</a> as an administrative county. In 2001, upon the completion of the County Hall, senior executive offices moved there from Parnell Square in Dublin city centre.\n</p><p>In June 2006, the <a href="/wiki/Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution" title="Royal National Lifeboat Institution">RNLI</a> Ireland officially opened its new all-Ireland headquarters at <a href="/wiki/Airside_Retail_Park" title="Airside Retail Park">Airside</a> Business Park, within greater Swords. It was officially opened by President <a href="/wiki/Mary_McAleese" title="Mary McAleese">Mary McAleese</a>. In attendance at the ceremony was <a href="/wiki/Admiral_(Royal_Navy)" title="Admiral (Royal Navy)">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Jock_Slater" title="Jock Slater">Sir Jock Slater</a>, <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">RN</a>, a former British <a href="/wiki/First_Sea_Lord" class="mw-redirect" title="First Sea Lord">First Sea Lord</a> then serving as Chairman of the Executive Committee of the RNLI.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Strategic_vision">Strategic vision</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Strategic vision">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Fingal County Council\'s "Strategic Vision" for Swords is reputedly to create a sustainable "new city". The council has referred to Swords as an "emerging city" and has projected that the population of Swords would rise towards 100,000 by the year 2035.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> The town is the seventh-largest urban area in the country, and the third-largest in <a href="/wiki/County_Dublin" title="County Dublin">County Dublin</a>, after Dublin City and <a href="/wiki/Tallaght" title="Tallaght">Tallaght</a>.\n</p><p>Swords Cultural Quarter Masterplan by Fingal County Council proposed to redevelop the centre of Swords surrounding the castle.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quality_of_life">Quality of life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Quality of life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In 2012, Swords was named the third best town in Ireland to live in. The survey conducted by Retail Excellence Ireland took into account safety, retail, dining, entertainment, events, car parking and overall attractiveness of the town.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Since the mid-1990s Swords has seen improvements in shop fronts, public buildings and footpaths and the restoration of <a href="/wiki/Swords_Castle" title="Swords Castle">Swords Castle</a>.\n</p><p>In 2003 the <i>Irish Business Against Litter</i> (IBAL) survey scored Swords the worst "litter blackspot" in the country.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Following improvements in litter levels, a 2011 survey declared Swords to be the second cleanest town in Ireland.<sup id="cite_ref-ibal.ie_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ibal.ie-21">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> In the 2019 survey, An Taisce, who carry out the surveys on behalf of IBAL, stated: \'A stellar showing for this large urban area. Swords is a model for others to follow.<sup id="cite_ref-2019_IBAL_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2019_IBAL-22">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">Geography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Geography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Landscape">Landscape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Landscape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Swords_1898.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Swords_1898.jpg/220px-Swords_1898.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="140" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Swords_1898.jpg/330px-Swords_1898.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Swords_1898.jpg/440px-Swords_1898.jpg 2x" data-file-width="497" data-file-height="317" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Swords_1898.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Main Street, Swords in 1940</div></div></div>\n<p>Swords is situated roughly in the centre of the modern county of Fingal and the ancient <a href="/wiki/Barony_(Ireland)" title="Barony (Ireland)">barony</a> of <a href="/wiki/Nethercross" title="Nethercross">Nethercross</a>.\n</p><p>The Ward River, coming from County Meath, runs west to east to near the centre of the town, and then turns to run north, before flowing into the Broad Meadow Water or Broadmeadow River to the east of the town, across the former northern road. A small stream joins the Ward near the town centre and the holy well.  The Broadmeadow, also flowing from Meath, borders the north of the town. It runs from <a href="/wiki/Dunshaughlin" title="Dunshaughlin">Dunshaughlin</a> in the west and across the north of Swords, before receiving the Ward and flowing into the wide Broadmeadow Estuary, then into the Irish Sea past Malahide.  The estuary is crossed by a railway embankment and bridge from Malahide.<sup id="cite_ref-TenDozenW_BM_and_Ward_Rvrs_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TenDozenW_BM_and_Ward_Rvrs-23">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Swords is surrounded by a protected green belt. Dublin Airport has prevented the town from expanding further south and the large Broadmeadow Estuary and Malahide beyond limit expansion further east. To the north and west of Swords there is sparsely-populated, relatively flat, farmland.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Townlands_and_baronies">Townlands and baronies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Townlands and baronies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The civil parish of Swords mainly lies in the ancient <a href="/wiki/Barony_(Ireland)" title="Barony (Ireland)">barony</a> of <a href="/wiki/Nethercross" title="Nethercross">Nethercross</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Nethercross_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nethercross-24">&#91;N 3&#93;</a></sup> Swords Demesne is the name of the <a href="/wiki/Townland" title="Townland">townland</a> in the heart of the urban town of Swords.<sup id="cite_ref-Swords_Demesne_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Swords_Demesne-25">&#91;N 4&#93;</a></sup> It is one of 58 such geographic units in the civil parish. However, a single parcel of land, 5 acres in extent, is situated in the barony of <a href="/wiki/Coolock_(barony)" title="Coolock (barony)">Coolock</a><sup id="cite_ref-Glebe_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Glebe-26">&#91;N 5&#93;</a></sup> as an <a href="/wiki/Exclave" class="mw-redirect" title="Exclave">exclave</a> of the civil parish proper.\n</p><p>There are 10 townlands in the <a href="/wiki/District_electoral_division" class="mw-redirect" title="District electoral division">electoral division</a> of Swords, which is not co-terminous with the civil parish.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Urban_layout">Urban layout</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Urban layout">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:SwordsMainStreetSouthfacing.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/SwordsMainStreetSouthfacing.jpg/220px-SwordsMainStreetSouthfacing.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/SwordsMainStreetSouthfacing.jpg/330px-SwordsMainStreetSouthfacing.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/SwordsMainStreetSouthfacing.jpg/440px-SwordsMainStreetSouthfacing.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:SwordsMainStreetSouthfacing.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Swords Main Street at Malahide Road junction</div></div></div>\n<p>The main retail area is located in the centre of the town, and includes Main Street, with the Pavilions and Swords Central combined shopping centres, and two smaller retail developments, Swords Plaza and Swords Town Mall.  Most civic facilities are also in this central area, with some subsidiary shopping and civic centres in surrounding housing areas.\n</p><p>The west of the urban area is mainly residential, with the neighbourhoods of <a href="/wiki/Applewood,_Swords" title="Applewood, Swords">Applewood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rathbeale,_Swords" title="Rathbeale, Swords">Rathbeale</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brackenstown,_Swords" title="Brackenstown, Swords">Brackenstown</a> to the north of the Ward River and <a href="/wiki/Knocksedan,_Swords" title="Knocksedan, Swords">Knocksedan</a>, River Valley, Rathingle and Boroimhe to the south side of the river.\n</p><p>The main business and industrial areas are located to the east of the town centre, along the R132 dual carriageway. These include Balheary Industrial Park, Swords Business Campus, Swords Business Park, and the Airside campus (Business Park, Retail Park and Motor Park). The neighbourhoods of Seatown, <a href="/wiki/Holywell,_Swords" title="Holywell, Swords">Holywell</a> and Drynam are also to the east of the town core.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Postal_designation">Postal designation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Postal designation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords has a postal address of County Dublin, and an <a href="/wiki/Eircode" class="mw-redirect" title="Eircode">eircode</a> "routing key" of K67.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">Climate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Climate">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The climate of Swords is, like the rest of Ireland, classified as a <a href="/wiki/Maritime_climate" class="mw-redirect" title="Maritime climate">maritime temperate climate</a> (<i>Cfb</i>) according to the <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="K\xc3\xb6ppen climate classification">K\xc3\xb6ppen climate classification</a> system.  It is mild and changeable with abundant rainfall and a lack of temperature extremes. The hottest months of the year are June, July and August with temperatures of around 17 \xe2\x80\x93 20 degrees. Swords gets rainfall all year round and the wettest months are October to January.\n</p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<div>\n<table class="wikitable mw-collapsible" style="width:100%; border-left-width:medium">3.9\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="14" style="text-align:center;font-size:95%;">Source: Met \xc3\x89ireann<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n</div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">Demographics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Demographics">edit</a><span Swords">Demographics of Swords</a></div>\n<table class="toccolours collapsible collapsed" style="width:22.2em;border-top-width:0;border-spacing: 0;float:right;clear:right;margin:0.5em 0 1em
