solid #bbbbbb">15,312</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px;border-bottom:1px solid #bbbbbb">+37.5%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">1991</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">17,705</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+15.6%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">1996</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">22,314</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+26.0%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">2002</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">27,175</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+21.8%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">2006</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">37,762</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+39.0%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">2011</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">42,738</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+13.2%</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>Swords has developed into one of the largest urban areas in Ireland. The town\'s population boom began in the 1970s with the construction of the sprawling Rivervalley Estate, then Ireland\'s largest private housing development, ahead of Kilnamanagh Estate in Tallaght North.  It continued during the 1990s and 2000s, with many new residents moving to the area due to its proximity to work at <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Airport" title="Dublin Airport">Dublin Airport</a> and various industrial estates.\n</p><p>At the 2011 census, the total urban population of greater Swords was 42,738.  This wider area of Swords had a population density in 2011 of 3765/km<sup>2</sup>, making it the most densely populated urban area in Ireland.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Fingal County Council has referred to Swords as an "Emerging City", and have suggested that the overall area\'s population may reach 100,000 by 2035.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Transport">Transport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Transport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Transport_in_Dublin" title="Transport in Dublin">Transport in Dublin</a></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Roads">Roads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Roads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:MonumentSwords.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/MonumentSwords.jpg/170px-MonumentSwords.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="302" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/MonumentSwords.jpg/255px-MonumentSwords.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/MonumentSwords.jpg/340px-MonumentSwords.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2304" data-file-height="4096" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:MonumentSwords.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>F\xc3\xa1ilte Sord 2018 sculpture</div></div></div>\n<p>Swords has good road links due to its proximity to Dublin city, which is the main focus for the Irish road network. The <a href="/wiki/M1_Motorway_(Republic_of_Ireland)" class="mw-redirect" title="M1 Motorway (Republic of Ireland)">M1</a> Dublin-Belfast motorway passes along the eastern edge of the town and is the main route to/from Dublin City, Drogheda, Dundalk, Newry and Belfast. The <a href="/wiki/M50_motorway_(Ireland)" title="M50 motorway (Ireland)">M50</a> Dublin semi-orbital motorway passes to the south of the town and provides connections with all of the other main roads out of Dublin (N2, N3, N4, N7, N81 and M11). The <a href="/wiki/R132_road_(Ireland)" title="R132 road (Ireland)">R132</a> dual-carriageway by-passes the centre of Swords, and runs south to Dublin Airport and north to Balbriggan. The proposed Swords Western Ring Road dual carriageway is due to run from the M1 at Lissenhall, north of Swords, along the western edge of Swords to the M2 motorway at Cherryhound. Other main roads from Swords include the <a href="/wiki/R106_road_(Ireland)" title="R106 road (Ireland)">R106</a> to Malahide and Portmarnock, <a href="/wiki/R108_road_(Ireland)" title="R108 road (Ireland)">R108</a> to Ballyboughal and Naul, <a href="/wiki/R125_road_(Ireland)" title="R125 road (Ireland)">R125</a> to Ashbourne and the M2 motorway, <a href="/wiki/R126_road_(Ireland)" title="R126 road (Ireland)">R126</a> to Donabate and Portrane and <a href="/wiki/R127_road_(Ireland)" title="R127 road (Ireland)">R127</a> to Lusk and Skerries.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bus">Bus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Bus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The town\'s Main Street is served by <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Bus" title="Dublin Bus">Dublin Bus</a> (and <a href="/wiki/Go-Ahead_Ireland" title="Go-Ahead Ireland">Go-Ahead Ireland</a>) routes 33, 33A, 33B, 33N, 41, 41B, 41C, 41X, 43, 102 and 142 as well as <a href="/wiki/Bus_%C3%89ireann" title="Bus \xc3\x89ireann">Bus \xc3\x89ireann</a> routes <a href="/wiki/Bus_%C3%89ireann_Route_101" title="Bus \xc3\x89ireann Route 101">101 and 101n</a>, and Swords Express routes 500, 500x, 501, 501x and 502. Buses operate between Swords and Dublin city centre approximately every 5 minutes throughout the day, through a combination of Dublin Bus routes 33, 41, 41B, 41C, 41X &amp; 43,<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> with a journey time of about an hour.  Swords Express<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> operate express services through the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Port_Tunnel" title="Dublin Port Tunnel">Dublin Port Tunnel</a> which take about 35 minutes. Other bus routes serving Swords include the 102 to <a href="/wiki/Malahide" title="Malahide">Malahide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portmarnock" title="Portmarnock">Portmarnock</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sutton,_Dublin" title="Sutton, Dublin">Sutton</a>, route 33b to <a href="/wiki/Donabate" title="Donabate">Donabate</a> and <a href="/wiki/Portrane" title="Portrane">Portrane</a>, routes 33 and 33a to <a href="/wiki/Lusk,_Dublin" title="Lusk, Dublin">Lusk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rush,_Dublin" title="Rush, Dublin">Rush</a>, <a href="/wiki/Skerries,_Dublin" title="Skerries, Dublin">Skerries</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Balbriggan" title="Balbriggan">Balbriggan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bus_%C3%89ireann" title="Bus \xc3\x89ireann">Bus \xc3\x89ireann</a> route 101 to <a href="/wiki/Balbriggan" title="Balbriggan">Balbriggan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Julianstown" title="Julianstown">Julianstown</a> and <a href="/wiki/Drogheda" title="Drogheda">Drogheda</a>. Connect Bus and Coach operate route H1 every 20 minutes between Dublin Airport and the Travelodge Hotel in Swords.\n</p><p>There are a number of long-distance bus services from the Atrium Road and coach park in Dublin Airport<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> to various locations throughout the country operated by Bus \xc3\x89ireann<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> and other private companies, including 50 daily services to <a href="/wiki/Belfast" title="Belfast">Belfast</a> (route 1/X2 &amp; Aircoach<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>), 12 to <a href="/wiki/Derry" title="Derry">Derry</a> (route 33 &amp; John Mc Ginley<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>), 11 to <a href="/wiki/Letterkenny" title="Letterkenny">Letterkenny</a> (route 32 &amp; John Mc Ginley), 9 to <a href="/wiki/Donegal_(town)" title="Donegal (town)">Donegal</a> (route 30), 3 to <a href="/wiki/Sligo" title="Sligo">Sligo</a> (route 23), 1 to <a href="/wiki/Ballina,_County_Mayo" title="Ballina, County Mayo">Ballina</a> (route 22), 52 to <a href="/wiki/Galway" title="Galway">Galway</a> (route 20, Citylink<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> &amp; gobus<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>), 14 to <a href="/wiki/Limerick" title="Limerick">Limerick</a> (route 12 &amp; JJ Kavanagh<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>), 24 to <a href="/wiki/Cork_(city)" title="Cork (city)">Cork</a> (GoB\xc3\xa9 &amp; Aircoach), 6 to Clonmel (JJ Kavanagh), 21 to <a href="/wiki/Waterford" title="Waterford">Waterford</a> (route 4/X4 &amp; JJ Kavanagh) and 31 to <a href="/wiki/Wexford" title="Wexford">Wexford</a> (route 2, Ardcavan<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> &amp; Wexford Bus<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rail">Rail</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Rail">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords has no railway services. The nearest railway stations are at <a href="/wiki/Malahide" title="Malahide">Malahide</a> and <a href="/wiki/Donabate" title="Donabate">Donabate</a>. Malahide is served by the frequent Dublin area rapid transit service to <a href="/wiki/Bray,_County_Wicklow" title="Bray, County Wicklow">Bray</a>, through the city centre. Both Malahide and Donabate are served by Dublin \xe2\x80\x93 <a href="/wiki/Drogheda" title="Drogheda">Drogheda</a> commuter services.\n</p><p>Swords is the only Dublin county town not to be served by rail, as <a href="/wiki/Tallaght" title="Tallaght">Tallaght</a> in <a href="/wiki/South_Dublin" title="South Dublin">South Dublin</a> is served by the <a href="/wiki/Luas" title="Luas">Luas</a> light rail system, and <a href="/wiki/D%C3%BAn_Laoghaire" title="D\xc3\xban Laoghaire">D\xc3\xban Laoghaire</a> is served by the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Area_Rapid_Transit" title="Dublin Area Rapid Transit">DART</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iarnr%C3%B3d_%C3%89ireann" title="Iarnr\xc3\xb3d \xc3\x89ireann">Irish Rail</a> services.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Metro">Metro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Metro">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:ThePlazaSwords.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/ThePlazaSwords.jpg/220px-ThePlazaSwords.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/ThePlazaSwords.jpg/330px-ThePlazaSwords.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/ThePlazaSwords.jpg/440px-ThePlazaSwords.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:ThePlazaSwords.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Plaza, Swords</div></div></div>\n<p>There are proposals for a light rapid transit line, the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Metro#Metro_North" class="mw-redirect" title="Dublin Metro">Metro North</a> line, to run from <a href="/wiki/St_Stephen%27s_Green" title="St Stephen&#39;s Green">St Stephen\'s Green</a> to Swords via the Mater Hospital, Drumcondra Railway Station, <a href="/wiki/Dublin_City_University" title="Dublin City University">Dublin City University</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ballymun" title="Ballymun">Ballymun</a> and Dublin Airport. In 2015, the Government announced that Metro North would be redesigned to a cheaper cost. Construction of the line was proposed to begin in 2021 and be completed by 2026.\n</p><p>Three stops have been proposed within or near Swords (at Estuary, Swords Central, Fosterstown) with another at the airport (between Terminals 1 and 2). A further three stops were originally proposed but were refused planning permission.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dublin_Airport">Dublin Airport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Dublin Airport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Dublin_Airport" title="Dublin Airport">Dublin Airport</a>, the busiest airport in Ireland, is located at Collinstown, several kilometres to the south of Swords. The airport has direct flights to Britain, Europe, North America, North Africa and the Middle East. In 2019, 32.9 million passenger journeys were recorded,<sup id="cite_ref-2019_air_figs_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2019_air_figs-40">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> and it is by far the busiest of the <a href="/wiki/Airports_in_the_Republic_of_Ireland_by_total_passenger_traffic" class="mw-redirect" title="Airports in the Republic of Ireland by total passenger traffic">airports by total passenger traffic</a> in Ireland. As of 2014, Dublin\xe2\x80\x93London was the world\'s second busiest international air route, behind Hong Kong\xe2\x80\x93Taipei.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Knocksedan_Heliport">Knocksedan Heliport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Knocksedan Heliport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Knocksedan Heliport is a private heliport on the western side of Swords, run by Celtic Helicopters. The heliport has four hangars and they provide a helicopter wash facility and Jet A1 Fuel.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Irish Helicopters also use the heliport. They provide aerial crane, filming and survey services, helicopter charter and maintenance, spraying and special project services.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Features_and_historical_attractions">Features and historical attractions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Features and historical attractions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Some historical attractions are listed below.  Many of these are promoted by Swords Historical Society.<sup id="cite_ref-Swords_Historical_Society_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Swords_Historical_Society-44">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swords_Castle">Swords Castle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Swords Castle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Swords_Castle" title="Swords Castle">Swords Castle</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:SwordsCastleMain.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/SwordsCastleMain.jpg/220px-SwordsCastleMain.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/SwordsCastleMain.jpg/330px-SwordsCastleMain.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/SwordsCastleMain.jpg/440px-SwordsCastleMain.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:SwordsCastleMain.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Swords Castle</div></div></div>\n<p>Swords Castle was built as the manorial residence of the 1st <a href="/wiki/Archbishop_of_Dublin_(Roman_Catholic)" title="Archbishop of Dublin (Roman Catholic)">Archbishop of Dublin</a>, John Comyn, around 1200 or a little later in Swords, just north of Dublin. It was never strong in the military sense, but covers a large pentagonal walled area of nearly 1.5 acres (6,000 m<sup>2</sup>) with a tower on the north and a gateway complex on the south. The adjoining chapel, built in the late thirteenth century, was probably used as the Archbishop\'s private oratory.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>Other buildings, recorded in an inquisition in 1326, have now vanished, including the great hall on the east side of the enclosure. The Archbishop abandoned Swords once a new palace was built at <a href="/wiki/Tallaght" title="Tallaght">Tallaght</a> in 1324. The stepped battlements suggest some form of occupancy during the fifteenth century, but by 1583, when briefly occupied by <a href="/wiki/Dutch_people" title="Dutch people">Dutch</a> <a href="/wiki/Protestants" class="mw-redirect" title="Protestants">Protestants</a>, it was described as "the quite spoiled old castle". It was used as a garden in the nineteenth century and sold after the <a href="/wiki/Church_of_Ireland" title="Church of Ireland">Church of Ireland</a> was disestablished.\n</p><p>Swords Castle has undergone restoration and is open as a tourist attraction. The castle was used as a film location for the production of TV series <a href="/wiki/The_Tudors" title="The Tudors">The Tudors</a> in spring 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span id="St._Colmcille.27s_Well"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="St._Colmcille\'s_Well">St. Colmcille\'s Well</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: St. Colmcille&#039;s Well">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>On Well Road, and also known as St. Columb\'s Well. In a locked chamber.  Reputed to be where Swords got its name when St. Colmcille blessed the well of clear water, \'Sord\' being the Irish for \'clear or pure\'.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:County_Dublin_-_Townparks_Holy_Well-St_Colmcilles_Well_-_20170925132515.jpg" class="image"><img alt="St Colmcilles Well" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/County_Dublin_-_Townparks_Holy_Well-St_Colmcilles_Well_-_20170925132515.jpg/220px-County_Dublin_-_Townparks_Holy_Well-St_Colmcilles_Well_-_20170925132515.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/County_Dublin_-_Townparks_Holy_Well-St_Colmcilles_Well_-_20170925132515.jpg/330px-County_Dublin_-_Townparks_Holy_Well-St_Colmcilles_Well_-_20170925132515.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/County_Dublin_-_Townparks_Holy_Well-St_Colmcilles_Well_-_20170925132515.jpg/440px-County_Dublin_-_Townparks_Holy_Well-St_Colmcilles_Well_-_20170925132515.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="2664" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:County_Dublin_-_Townparks_Holy_Well-St_Colmcilles_Well_-_20170925132515.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>St Colmcilles Well</div></div></div>\n<h3><span id="St._Columba.27s_Church.2C_Belfry_.26_Round_Tower"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="St._Columba\'s_Church,_Belfry_&amp;_Round_Tower">St. Columba\'s Church, Belfry &amp; Round Tower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: St. Columba&#039;s Church, Belfry &amp; Round Tower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:StColmcillesTower.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/StColmcillesTower.jpg/220px-StColmcillesTower.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/StColmcillesTower.jpg/330px-StColmcillesTower.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/StColmcillesTower.jpg/440px-StColmcillesTower.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:StColmcillesTower.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>St. Columba\'s Church and round tower</div></div></div>\n<p>The round tower is the surviving remnant of St. Colmcille\'s monastic settlement. The only remaining relic of the medieval church is its belfry, from c. 1300, which is open to the public in the summertime. The original church is said to have fallen into ruin sometime in the seventeenth century. The new church of early Gothic style was built in 1811 on the foundations of the old.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> The Sexton\'s Lodge was built in 1870. The body of <a href="/wiki/Brian_Boru" title="Brian Boru">Brian Boru</a> was said to have been brought there in 1014 to be waked after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Clontarf" title="Battle of Clontarf">Battle of Clontarf</a>, while on the way to be buried in <a href="/wiki/Armagh" title="Armagh">Armagh</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_Borough_School">Old Borough School</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Old Borough School">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:StColumbasCofI.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/StColumbasCofI.jpg/220px-StColumbasCofI.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/StColumbasCofI.jpg/330px-StColumbasCofI.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/StColumbasCofI.jpg/440px-StColumbasCofI.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:StColumbasCofI.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>St Columba\' s Church of Ireland church and graveyard</div></div></div>\n<p>Located on Main Street, the building was designed by the architect Francis Johnston. In 2015, <a href="/wiki/Wetherspoon" class="mw-redirect" title="Wetherspoon">Wetherspoon</a> bought the premises, and now operate The Old Borough as a public house.\n</p>\n<h3><span id="St._Colmcille.E2.80.99s_RC_Church"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="St._Colmcille\xe2\x80\x99s_RC_Church">St. Colmcille\xe2\x80\x99s RC Church</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: St. Colmcille\xe2\x80\x99s RC Church">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:StColmcills.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/StColmcills.jpg/220px-StColmcills.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/StColmcills.jpg/330px-StColmcills.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/StColmcills.jpg/440px-StColmcills.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:StColmcills.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>St Colmcille\'s RC Church</div></div></div>\n<p>On Chapel Lane, a pre-Catholic Emancipation church built in 1827 on a site donated by James Taylor of Swords House. The graveyard contains the headstones of nationalist politician <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Kettle" title="Andrew Kettle">Andrew Kettle</a>, who was known as "Parnell\xe2\x80\x99s Righthand Man."\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Courthouse">Courthouse</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Courthouse">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:CourtHouseSwords.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/CourtHouseSwords.jpg/220px-CourtHouseSwords.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/CourtHouseSwords.jpg/330px-CourtHouseSwords.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/CourtHouseSwords.jpg/440px-CourtHouseSwords.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:CourtHouseSwords.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Swords Courthouse</div></div></div>\n<p>Designed by Alexander Tate, Swords Courthouse is located on North Street and was built in 1845 in Classical style.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Mayors">Lord Mayors</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Lord Mayors">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Founded in 1668, the 350 year old Lord mayors is a Swords landmark. The thatched roof pub is the oldest structure in the village.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The Lord mayors closed for business in April 2019<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> leaving the premises vacant, with some locals questioning the plan to build 172 apartments on the site of the historic structure.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fingal_County_Hall">Fingal County Hall</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Fingal County Hall">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Fingal_County_Hall.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Fingal_County_Hall.jpg/220px-Fingal_County_Hall.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="163" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Fingal_County_Hall.jpg/330px-Fingal_County_Hall.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Fingal_County_Hall.jpg/440px-Fingal_County_Hall.jpg 2x" data-file-width="639" data-file-height="473" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Fingal_County_Hall.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Fingal County Hall</div></div></div>\n<p>The modern <a href="/wiki/County_Hall,_Swords" title="County Hall, Swords">Fingal County Hall</a>, by Bucholz McEvoy architects, is located at the northern end of Main Street. It is built on the site of Swords House, the home of the Norman family, the Taylors of Swords. Records show the family arrived there in the 13th century and built a \'Mansion House\' in 1403.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Leisure_and_cultural_facilities">Leisure and cultural facilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Leisure and cultural facilities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swords_library">Swords library</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Swords library">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords library, located on Rathbeale Road, offers typical library services and runs cultural activities for children and adults.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Historical_society">Historical society</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Historical society">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords Historical Society, founded in 1982, is supported by volunteers who have worked to record, promote and preserve the heritage of the greater Swords area. The society\'s Museum and Heritage Centre at the Carnegie Library on North Street is run by volunteers and is open on weekday afternoons. The society\'s oral history project has produced an annual \'Swords Voices\' publication, which chronicles the memories of local people.<sup id="cite_ref-Swords_Historical_Society_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Swords_Historical_Society-44">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ward_River_Valley_Park">Ward River Valley Park</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Ward River Valley Park">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The Ward River Valley Park is a linear park on the banks of the Ward River approaching town. It covers an area of 89 ha. (220 acres) between Swords town centre and Knocksedan Bridge. Features include some 12th-century fortifications, woodland habitats, wetlands and rolling grassland. There are viewing points, picnic sites, sports pitches and tennis courts.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span id="Swords_Town_Park_.28with_Swords_Castle.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Swords_Town_Park_(with_Swords_Castle)">Swords Town Park (with Swords Castle)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Swords Town Park (with Swords Castle)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:TownParkNorth.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/TownParkNorth.jpg/220px-TownParkNorth.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/TownParkNorth.jpg/330px-TownParkNorth.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/TownParkNorth.jpg/440px-TownParkNorth.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:TownParkNorth.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Swords Town Park, with Ward River on left</div></div></div>\n<p>Swords Town Park is a small park situated in the centre of the town of Swords, along the Ward River.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> It has tennis courts and a playground. Swords Castle lies within the park. It is the former residence of the Archbishop of Dublin and it is the only fortified residence of the Archbishop to survive in a reasonable state today (see above).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Balheary_Park">Balheary Park</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Balheary Park">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Balheary Park is north of the town centre near the confluence of the Broadmeadow River and the Ward River, which flow to the northern and southern edges of the park. It meets Swords Business Campus / Balheary Business Park on three sides, and has some playing pitches which are used by Fingallians GAA club. In mid-2006, Fingal County Council built a <a href="/wiki/Skatepark" title="Skatepark">skatepark</a> and adjoining basketball courts/football court in Balheary Park. The park contains a bowl, a vertwall, a spine, some <a href="/wiki/Quarterpipe" class="mw-redirect" title="Quarterpipe">quarterpipes</a>, and a section of boxes in the middle of the park.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Broadmeadow_River_Linear_Park">Broadmeadow River Linear Park</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Broadmeadow River Linear Park">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The Broadmeadow Linear Park is a small park north of Applewood along the Broadmeadow River. Fingal County Council plan to extend the park eastwards to Balheary Park and westwards into the proposed Swords Regional Park.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="National_Show_Centre">National Show Centre</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: National Show Centre">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>A little south of Swords, the National Show Centre is a modern exhibition and conference venue near to <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Airport" title="Dublin Airport">Dublin Airport</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> It is owned by the Irish Kennel Club, who use it as their main venue for dog shows in Ireland.\n</p><p>The National Show Centre is used as the count centre during elections for the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Fingal_(D%C3%A1il_constituency)" title="Dublin Fingal (D\xc3\xa1il constituency)">Dublin Fingal</a> constituency.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Boxing">Boxing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Boxing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords Boxing Club is based at Sluagh Hall, a former military facility which is shared with <a href="/wiki/Fingallians_GAA" title="Fingallians GAA">Fingallians GAA</a> clbu.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Fingal Boxing Academy, which is affiliated with the <a href="/wiki/Irish_Amateur_Boxing_Association" class="mw-redirect" title="Irish Amateur Boxing Association">Irish Amateur Boxing Association</a> and located in Rivervalley, Swords, was the first boxing club in Ireland to train female boxers and has trained several national champions.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="GAA">GAA</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: GAA">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>There are three Gaelic Athletic Association clubs local to Swords, and one more with pitches. These include <a href="/wiki/Fingallians" class="mw-redirect" title="Fingallians">Fingallians</a> (based at Lawless Memorial Park), St. Finian\'s (Rivervalley), and <a href="/wiki/St._Colmcille%27s_(Balheary)" title="St. Colmcille&#39;s (Balheary)">St Colmcille\'s</a> (Holybanks, Glen Ellan Road in the <a href="/wiki/Applewood,_Swords" title="Applewood, Swords">Applewood</a> neighbourhood).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Golf">Golf</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Golf">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>There are several golf courses close to the town, namely Swords Open Golf Course, Forrest Little Golf Club, Roganstown Golf and Country Club and Balheary "Par 3" Golf Course. There are also several driving ranges in the area with the Drynam Golf Centre being the first driving range in Ireland with automated tees.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rugby">Rugby</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Rugby">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Swords_RFC" title="Swords RFC">Swords RFC</a> are a <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">rugby union</a> team playing in Division 3 of the <a href="/wiki/Leinster_League" title="Leinster League">Leinster League</a>. The club is based out of ALSAA Sport Complex beside the airport and has 2 Men\'s teams and 1 Women\'s team. All teams train Tuesdays and Thursdays between July and April.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Soccer">Soccer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Soccer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords_Celtic_F.C.&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Swords Celtic F.C. (page does not exist)">Swords Celtic</a>, established in 1962, fields DDSL, NDSL, LSL, and MGL schoolboy and schoolgirl teams.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> The main pitch and clubhouse are located at Balheary, Swords and includes dressing rooms an eleven-aside and two seven-a-side pitches with flood lights.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>Swords Manor FC, established in 1995, fields NDSL, DDSL, MGL, and UCFL schoolboy and schoolgirl teams.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> The main pitch and clubhouse are located on the Brackenstown Road.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>River Valley Rangers AFC was established in 1981. It fields NDSL schoolboy/girl teams and its pitch and clubhouse are located in Ridgewood Park.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>Columbas Rovers FC was established in 2002. It uses the ALSAA sports centre near the airport.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>A former club, Swords Rovers FC (founded in 1993), was disbanded in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_sports">Other sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Other sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Fingal Orienteers have created <a href="/wiki/Orienteering" title="Orienteering">orienteering</a> maps of the Ward River Valley park, and the surrounding estates of Swords Manor, Brackenstown, River Valley and Knocksedan, and regularly hold events in the area.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> \n</p><p>Racquet sports clubs include Forest Badminton Club, River Valley Badminton Club, and Swords Tennis Club (based at Swords Town Park). Swords Hockey Club is a ladies club based in ALSAA Sports Grounds. There is also a basketball club in Swords.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>There are also several Taekwondo, kickboxing, karate, and judo clubs in the area.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fingal_Horticultural_Show">Fingal Horticultural Show</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Fingal Horticultural Show">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The Fingal Horticultural Society holds their annual flower show in Swords every August.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> It includes competition classes in Cut Flowers, Hanging Baskets, Pot Plants, Flower Arranging, Fruit, Vegetables, Cookery, Wine Making, Photography, Painting and Handcrafts, as well as special classes for children. The Fingal Horticultural Society also hold an annual Garden Competition, Allotment Competition and Pub Frontage Competition in Swords.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Flavours_of_Fingal_Agricultural_Show">Flavours of Fingal Agricultural Show</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Flavours of Fingal Agricultural Show">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The first Flavours of Fingal Show took place in July 2012 in Newbridge House near Donabate. The farm section of the two-day show featured a program of livestock and sheep competitions, equestrian contests and other agricultural displays. Separately, the walled garden of Newbridge House hosted the food producers section of the show. During the festival, family and musical entertainment, walks and other events were held.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dog_shows">Dog shows</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Dog shows">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In 2012 over 80 dog shows were held in the National Show Centre,<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> including the Celtic Winners Dog Show, held on St. Patrick\'s Day.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research" title="Wikipedia:No original research"><span title="The material near this tag possibly contains original research. (July 2020)">original research?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fingal_10k_Road_Race">Fingal 10k Road Race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Fingal 10k Road Race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The first Fingal 10k Road Race took place on 22 July 2012 on the roads around Swords. It was part of the Dublin Race Series, a series which culminates in the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Marathon" title="Dublin Marathon">Dublin Marathon</a>. Over 4200 people entered the first race, and the event has since been run annually.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">Economy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Economy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:PavilionsSwords.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/PavilionsSwords.jpg/220px-PavilionsSwords.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/PavilionsSwords.jpg/330px-PavilionsSwords.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/PavilionsSwords.jpg/440px-PavilionsSwords.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:PavilionsSwords.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pavilions Shopping Centre, Swords</div></div></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Retail">Retail</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Retail">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords is the home to a large retail and business park called <a href="/wiki/Airside_Retail_Park" title="Airside Retail Park">Airside Retail and Business Park</a>, on the southern fringe of the town, hosting many employers, including the European Headquarters of <a href="/wiki/Kellogg%27s" title="Kellogg&#39;s">Kellogg\'s</a>. <a href="/wiki/Ingersoll_Rand" title="Ingersoll Rand">Ingersoll Rand</a> also has its corporate headquarters in the Airside Business Park.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> East of the town, running parallel to Swords bypass, lies the large Swords Business Park, where <a href="/wiki/The_Hertz_Corporation" title="The Hertz Corporation">The Hertz Corporation</a> have a Shared Services Centre.\n</p><p>Swords also has a large shopping centre, the <a href="/wiki/Swords_Pavilions" title="Swords Pavilions">Pavilions Swords</a>, off the R132, which has a multi-screen cinema and branches of <a href="/wiki/SuperValu_(Ireland)" title="SuperValu (Ireland)">SuperValu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dunnes_Stores" title="Dunnes Stores">Dunnes Stores</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Aviation">Aviation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Aviation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords is the closest town to <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Airport" title="Dublin Airport">Dublin Airport</a> and the airport has provided a lot of employment to the area. In 2011 the airport handled over 18.7 million passengers and served over 171 routes with 62 airlines.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> The airport serves as an operating base for <a href="/wiki/Aer_Lingus" title="Aer Lingus">Aer Lingus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aer_Lingus_Regional" title="Aer Lingus Regional">Aer Lingus Regional</a>, <a href="/wiki/Air_Contractors" class="mw-redirect" title="Air Contractors">Air Contractors</a>, <a href="/wiki/CityJet" title="CityJet">CityJet</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ryanair" title="Ryanair">Ryanair</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thomson_Airways" class="mw-redirect" title="Thomson Airways">Thomson Airways</a>, and as a maintenance base for Aer Lingus, CityJet, Dublin Aerospace,<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Eirtech Aviation,<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Etihad_Airways" title="Etihad Airways">Etihad Airways</a><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> and Ryanair.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Irish_Aviation_Authority" title="Irish Aviation Authority">Irish Aviation Authority</a><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> operate the Dublin Air Traffic Control Centre on the airport.\n</p><p>The headquarters of the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Airport_Authority" class="mw-redirect" title="Dublin Airport Authority">Dublin Airport Authority</a> and Ireland\'s four largest airlines are located in or near Swords. The <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Airport_Authority" class="mw-redirect" title="Dublin Airport Authority">Dublin Airport Authority</a>, who manage Dublin, Cork and Shannon Airports, employ over 3,000 people and have their headquarters on the airport campus.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Aer Lingus,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Ireland\'s flag carrier, have their headquarters on the Dublin Airport campus. CityJet, part of the <a href="/wiki/Air_France-KLM" class="mw-redirect" title="Air France-KLM">Air France-KLM</a> group, has its headquarters in Swords Business Campus<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> and Air Contractors, part of the <a href="/wiki/ASL_Aviation" class="mw-redirect" title="ASL Aviation">ASL Aviation</a> group, has its head office on the Malahide Road in Swords.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> In 2014, <a href="/wiki/Ryanair" title="Ryanair">Ryanair</a> moved into a new \xe2\x82\xac20m, 100,000 sq ft Dublin Head Office in Airside Business Park.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> The building was officially opened in April 2014.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Logistics">Logistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Logistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In 2007 <a href="/wiki/Tesco_Ireland" title="Tesco Ireland">Tesco Ireland</a> opened their new \xe2\x82\xac70 million distribution centre in Lanestown, between Swords and Donabate. With a building footprint of over 68,000&#160;m<sup>2</sup> and a total volume of 1.55&#160;million&#160;m<sup>2</sup> the Tesco Ireland distribution centre is the largest building on the island of Ireland and one of the 10 <a href="/wiki/List_of_largest_buildings_in_the_world" class="mw-redirect" title="List of largest buildings in the world">largest building in the world</a>. The building is over half a kilometre long and could fit 16 jumbo jets. It has 106 loading bays and supplies 106 stores up to 6 times a day.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pharmaceutical">Pharmaceutical</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Pharmaceutical">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords is the home to several international chemical producers and pharmaceutical giants, including Opec. <a href="/wiki/Merck_Sharp_%26_Dohme" class="mw-redirect" title="Merck Sharp &amp; Dohme">Merck Sharp &amp; Dohme</a> (formally Organnon) employ over 500 people in their facility in Drynam, which manufactures women\'s health, anaesthesiology and mental health products.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Bristol_Myers_Squibb" title="Bristol Myers Squibb">Bristol Myers Squibb</a> employ over 400 people in their Swords Laboratories bulk pharmaceutical plant on Watery Lane.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Lonza_Group" title="Lonza Group">Lonza Group</a> employ 45 people in their European manufacturing facility for personal care and industrial biocides, also on Watery Lane.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Food_and_horticulture">Food and horticulture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Food and horticulture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Swords is located in the centre of Fingal and is surrounded by farms growing crops like potatoes, wheat and barley. However, unlike the rest of Fingal, a lot of the food distributed from Swords has been imported from abroad.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> As of 2018, FoodCentral (marketed as "Ireland\'s national food park") was being developed south-west of Swords.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The Keeling\'s Group, who employ over 1700 people, have their headquarters in FoodCentral and use a lot of land around Swords.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> The Keeling\'s Farms division annually grow 2,500 tonnes of soft fruits/berries from 5 hectares of glasshouse, tunnel and field crops in Swords. They grow <a href="/wiki/Bramley_apple" title="Bramley apple">Bramley apples</a> in 139 acres of orchards and lettuce in 8 acres of glasshouses. Their glasshouses also produce 1,500 tonnes of red, orange, yellow and green peppers annually.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Keeling\'s also operate a large banana ripening facility for Chiquita which ripens over 3 million bananas each week. They also have separate ripening rooms for other fruits.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Total Produce, Ireland\'s largest agribusiness<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> operates two facilities in Swords.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> Its facility in Swords Business Park includes a distribution and ripening centre for Fyffes<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> Cape, Outspan, Green Ace and TOP Fruit products. Their "Uniplumo" facility on the Rathbeale Road,<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> has 46,000 square metres of glasshouses for growing plants, flowers and tomatoes.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Primary">Primary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Primary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The town is served by more than 10 <a href="/wiki/Education_in_the_Republic_of_Ireland#Types_of_school" title="Education in the Republic of Ireland">primary schools</a>. These include several <a href="/wiki/Gaelscoil" title="Gaelscoil">gaelscoils</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> a number of <a href="/wiki/Educate_Together" title="Educate Together">Educate Together</a> schools,<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> and mixed and gender-specific <a href="/wiki/National_school_(Ireland)" title="National school (Ireland)">national schools</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> The latter includes both <a href="/wiki/Church_of_Ireland" title="Church of Ireland">Church of Ireland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" class="mw-redirect" title="Roman Catholic">Roman Catholic</a> schools.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> A number of other primary schools are in planning or under construction.<sup id="cite_ref-Proposed_Mooretown_Primary_Schools_98-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Proposed_Mooretown_Primary_Schools-98">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Secondary">Secondary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Secondary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The secondary schools serving the town include Loreto College (all-girls school, River Valley),<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> Col\xc3\xa1iste Choilm C.B.S. (all-boys school, Dublin Road),<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Fingal Community College (Seatown Road),<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> St. Finian\'s Community College (Castlefarm),<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> and Swords Community College (Rathbeale Road)<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_level_and_further_education">Third level and further education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Third level and further education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Land has been reserved for a potential university campus at Lissenhall in north Swords.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers"><span title="The date of the event predicted near this tag has passed. (December 2020)">needs update</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>The National Learning Network, Fingal Adult Education Service and Swords Youthreach each have a presence in the area.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> \n</p><p>There is also the Fingal Adult Literacy and Education Centre<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">Religion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Religion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<table class="wikitable" style="margin:0;">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th>Population by religion (Census 2011)<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup></th>\n<th>Persons\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Roman Catholic</td>\n<td>34,021\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Orthodox (Greek, Coptic, Russian)</td>\n<td>1,335\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Church of Ireland, England, Anglican, Episcopalian</td>\n<td>944\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Apostolic or Pentecostal</td>\n<td>201\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Presbyterian</td>\n<td>195\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Other Christian religion</td>\n<td>454\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<th>Total Christian religions</th>\n<th>37,150\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Muslim (Islamic)</td>\n<td>579\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Other stated religions</td>\n<td>1,003\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>No religion</td>\n<td>3,006\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Not stated</td>\n<td>1,000\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<th>Total Population</th>\n<th>42,738\n</th></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Christianity">Christianity</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Christianity">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Roman Catholicism is the predominant religion in Swords. The town has six <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" class="mw-redirect" title="Roman Catholic">Roman Catholic</a> churches. St. Colmcille\'s, the Church of the Visitation and Our Lady Queen of Heaven are all within Swords parish.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> St. Cronan\'s and St. Finian\'s each belong to distinct parishes, while the Church of the Immaculate Conception lies within Donabate parish.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>There are also a further eight Christian churches and a retreat centre.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> These include St. Columba\'s <a href="/wiki/Church_of_Ireland" title="Church of Ireland">Church of Ireland</a> church on Church Road,<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Association_of_Baptist_Churches_in_Ireland" title="Association of Baptist Churches in Ireland">Baptist</a> churches which meet in St. Finian\'s Community College and at Seatown West.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Other Protestant and evangelical communities include the Apostolic Faith Church and Churchtown Trust.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Syriac_Orthodox_Church" title="Syriac Orthodox Church">Syriac Orthodox Church</a> meets as the St. Ignatius Jacobite Congregation in St Columba\'s Church of Ireland church.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jehovah%27s_Witnesses" title="Jehovah&#39;s Witnesses">Jehovah\'s Witnesses</a> meet at a <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_Hall" title="Kingdom Hall">Kingdom Hall</a> on Kettles Lane.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Islam">Islam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Swords,_Dublin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Islam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The Dublin Welfare Society manage a makeshift mosque in a Swords industrial estate<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Local_politicians">Local politicians</span><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Swords is part of the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_Fingal_(D%C3%A1il_constituency)" title="Dublin Fingal (D\xc3\xa1il constituency)">Dublin Fingal</a> constituency. href="#cite_note-126">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Eleanor_Ambrose" title="Eleanor Ambrose">Eleanor Ambrose</a>, Catholic heiress, is from Swords.</li>\n<li><a
